2.4.4 Formål med lenke (3 avvik)
Testregel 2.4.4 (2.4.4 - Nivå A)
MODERATE

Link text is a URL

<a href="https://www.telenor.no/kundeservice/mobil/problemer/#dekning">https://www.telenor.no/kundeservice/mobil/problemer/#dekning</a>
Replace URL with descriptive text that explains the link destination
Testregel 2.4.4 (2.4.4 - Nivå A)
MINOR

Link text has redundant phrase: 'Gå til hjelpesider'

<a class="tn-link text-l neutral" data-v-0082dc76="" data-v-9b029b67="" href="/kundeservice/" tabindex="0" title="Gå til hjelpesider"><!-- --><span data-v-0082dc76=""><!--[-->Gå til hjelpesider<!--]--
Remove 'link to' or similar - screen readers already announce it as a link

3.3.2 Ledetekster eller instruksjoner (1 avvik)
Testregel 3.3.2 (3.3.2 - Nivå A)
CRITICAL

Form input only has placeholder, no proper label

<input autocomplete="off" class="search-input" data-v-9b021b29="" id="search" name="q" placeholder="Søk" type="text" value=""/>
Add a <label> element with for attribute, or aria-label. Placeholder disappears when typing.

Add a skip link at the start of the page: <a href='#main'>Hopp til hovedinnhold</a>

MODERATE

Heading level skipped: h2 to h4

MODERATE

2.4.4 Formål med lenke (2 avvik)
Testregel 2.4.4 (2.4.4 - Nivå A)
MINOR

Link text has redundant phrase: 'Gå til hjelpesider'

<a class="tn-link text-l neutral" data-v-0082dc76="" data-v-9b029b67="" href="/kundeservice/" tabindex="0" title="Gå til hjelpesider"><!-- --><span data-v-0082dc76=""><!--[-->Gå til hjelpesider<!--]--
Remove 'link to' or similar - screen readers already announce it as a link
Testregel 2.4.4 (2.4.4 - Nivå A)
MINOR

Link text has redundant phrase: 'Gå til hjelpesider'

<a class="tn-link text-l neutral" data-v-0082dc76="" data-v-9b029b67="" href="/kundeservice/" tabindex="0" title="Gå til hjelpesider"><!-- --><span data-v-0082dc76=""><!--[-->Gå til hjelpesider<!--]--

3.3.2 Ledetekster eller instruksjoner (1 avvik)
Testregel 3.3.2 (3.3.2 - Nivå A)
CRITICAL

Form input only has placeholder, no proper label

<input autocomplete="off" class="search-input" data-v-9b021b29="" id="search" name="q" placeholder="Søk" type="text" value=""/>
Add a <label> element with for attribute, or aria-label. Placeholder disappears when typing.

<a href="https://www.telenor.no/om/personvern/folkeregisteret/">Les mer</a>
Use descriptive text that indicates where the link goes (e.g., 'Read more about products' instead of 'Read more')
Testregel 2.4.4 (2.4.4 - Nivå A)

Link text is a URL

<a href="https://www.telenor.no/privat/">www.telenor.no</a>

CRITICAL

Link has no accessible name (empty link)

<a alt="Share on X" class="button l secondary icon-only" data-href="https://twitter.com/share?url=https://www.telenor.no/om/personvern/" data-v-c7c37f7c="" data-v-dc567de2="" href="https://twitter.com
Add text content, aria-label, or image with alt text

3.3.2 Ledetekster eller instruksjoner (1 avvik)
Testregel 3.3.2 (3.3.2 - Nivå A)
CRITICAL

Form input only has placeholder, no proper label

<input autocomplete="off" class="search-input" data-v-9b021b29="" id="search" name="q" placeholder="Søk" type="text" value=""/>
Add a <label> element with for attribute, or aria-label. Placeholder disappears when typing.
2.4.1 Hopp over blokker (1 avvik)
Testregel 2.4.1 (2.4.1 - Nivå A)
MODERATE

Page has no skip link to bypass navigation

<body>
Add a skip link at the start of the page: <a href='#main'>Hopp til hovedinnhold</a>
